		i;1;CurTable.Out.MARKETS_Table.size()-1;1
			#If
			CurTable.Out.MARKETS_Table.get(i).get('MARKETS')==currency
				#Continue
				
			#Else
				#Action;#Dialog;#AppConnection;#MARKETS_Table
				DialogFill;'AddInstruments';Connection;Do.click(0,i)


			#EndIf

		#EndFor

	//Instrument
		#Id;#Action;#Dialog;#AppConnection;#INSTRUMENT_NAME_Table
		InstrTable;DialogFill;'AddInstruments';Connection;Do.getTable()
		
		#For;#From;#To;#Step
		i;0;InstrTable.Out.INSTRUMENT_NAME_Table.size()-1;1
			#If
			InstrTable.Out.INSTRUMENT_NAME_Table.get(i).get('INSTRUMENT_NAME')==currency+' '+Instrument
				#Id;#Action;#Dialog;#AppConnection;#INSTRUMENT_NAME_Table
				Indicator;DialogFill;'AddInstruments';Connection;Do.getValue(0,i)

				#If
				Indicator.Out.INSTRUMENT_NAME_Table=='true'
					#Break
				
				#Else
					#Action;#Dialog;#AppConnection;#INSTRUMENT_NAME_Table
					DialogFill;'AddInstruments';Connection;Do.click(0,i)

				#EndIf
				
			#EndIf

		#EndFor
		
		#Action;#Dialog;#AppConnection;#Save
		DialogFill;'AddInstruments';Connection;Do.click()

	#EndSubCase

	#Id;#SubCase;#Connection;#Instrument;#currency
	SelectInstrumentX;Select instrument by cur n name in tree;Connection;Instrument;currency
		#Action;#Dialog;#AppConnection;#MARKETS_Table
		DialogFill;'AddInstruments';Connection;Do.click(0,1)

		#Id;#Action;#Dialog;#AppConnection;#MARKETS_Table
		CurTable;DialogFill;'AddInstruments';Connection;Do.getRowIndexes(new StringCondition('MARKETS', currency), null)

		#Action;#Status
		Print;CurTable.Out.MARKETS_Table

		#Id;#Action;#Dialog;#AppConnection;#MARKETS_Table
		CurIndicator;DialogFill;'AddInstruments';Connection;Do.getValue(0,InstrTable.Out.MARKETS_Table)
		
		#If
		CurIndicator.Out.MARKETS_Table=='false'
			#Action;#Dialog;#AppConnection;#MARKETS_Table
			DialogFill;'AddInstruments';Connection;Do.click(0,i)

		#EndIf

		#Action;#Dialog;#AppConnection;#MARKETS_Table
		DialogFill;'AddInstruments';Connection;Do.click(0,CurTable.Out.MARKETS_Table)

		#Id;#Action;#Dialog;#AppConnection;#INSTRUMENT_NAME_Table
		InstrTable;DialogFill;'AddInstruments';Connection;Do.getRowIndexes(new StringCondition('INSTRUMENT_NAME', Instrument), null)
		
		#Id;#Action;#Dialog;#AppConnection;#INSTRUMENT_NAME_Table
		InstrIndicator;DialogFill;'AddInstruments';Connection;Do.getValue(0,InstrTable.Out.INSTRUMENT_NAME_Table)
		
		#If
		InstrIndicator.Out.INSTRUMENT_NAME_Table=='false'
			#Action;#Dialog;#AppConnection;#INSTRUMENT_NAME_Table
			DialogFill;'AddInstruments';Connection;Do.click(0,i)

		#EndIf
				
		#Action;#Dialog;#AppConnection;#Save
		DialogFill;'AddInstruments';Connection;Do.click()

	#EndSubCase

	#Id;#SubCase
	Disconnect;Disconnect the ethernet
		#Action;#Command
		Execute;'netsh interface set interface "Ethernet" DISABLED'
		
		#Action;#Command
		Execute;'netsh interface set interface "Ethernet 4" DISABLED'
				
		#Action;#Text;#Notifier
		Show;'Ethernet" DISABLED';Notifier.Success

	#EndSubCase
	
	#Id;#SubCase
	Connect;Connect the ethernet
		#Action;#Command
		Execute;'netsh interface set interface "Ethernet" ENABLED'
		
		#Action;#Command
		Execute;'netsh interface set interface "Ethernet 4" ENABLED'
		
		#RepOff;#Action;#Text;#Notifier
		1;Show;'Ethernet" ENABLED';Notifier.Success

		#RepOff;#Action;#Time
		1;Wait;5000
		
	#EndSubCase
	
	#Id;#SubCase;#Time
	Reconnect;Reconnect the ethernet;Time
		#Action;#Command
		Execute;'netsh interface set interface "Ethernet" DISABLED'
		
		#Action;#Command
		Execute;'netsh interface set interface "Ethernet 4" DISABLED'
		
		#RepOff;#Action;#Text;#Notifier
		1;Show;'Ethernet" DISABLED';Notifier.Success

		#RepOff;#Action;#Time
		1;Wait;Time
		
		#Action;#Command
		Execute;'netsh interface set interface "Ethernet" ENABLED'
		
		#Action;#Command
		Execute;'netsh interface set interface "Ethernet 4" ENABLED'
		
		#RepOff;#Action;#Text;#Notifier
		1;Show;'Ethernet" ENABLED';Notifier.Success

		#RepOff;#Action;#Time
		1;Wait;5000
		
	#EndSubCase

	#Id;#SubCase;#Connection
	Confirm;Input Confirm;Connection
		#Id;#IgnoreErr;#Action;#Dialog;#AppConnection;#BTN
		ok;1;DialogFill;'Confirm';Connection;Do.use(0).click()

		#Return
		ok.Result
		
	#EndSubCase

	#Id;#SubCase;#Connection
	Logout;Logout user;Connection
		#Id;#Action;#Dialog;#AppConnection;#Close
		Close;DialogFill;'Level1';Connection;Do.push()

		#Id;#IgnoreErr;#Action;#Dialog;#AppConnection;#BTN

		#Return
		ok.Result

		APPNUM;ApplicationStop;Connection


	#EndSubCase

				#Call;#Side;#Priority;#Trader;#Connection;#Role
				DeskReg.Repost;ORD.Out[Count].Side;ORD.Out[Count].Priority;ORD.Out[Count].Trader;Connection;ORD.Out[Count].Role


			#Case
			'Trade' // Trade
				#Call
				DeskReg.Trade


			#Case
			'ClosePrivate' // Close Private Phase
				#Call;#Connection
				DeskReg.ClosePrivate;Connection


			#Case
			'ClosePublic' // Close Public Phase
				#Call;#Connection
				DeskReg.ClosePublic;Connection


			#Case
			'CompleteWorkup' // Complete Trade
				#Call;#Connection
				DeskReg.CompleteWorkup;Connection


			#Case
			'ErrorTrade' // Trade
				#Call;#Connection
				DeskReg.ErrorWorkup;Connection

		//Checks
			#Case
			'CheckWorkup' // Check the Book
				#Call;#Priority;#Connection;#Instrument;#currency
				DeskReg.CheckWorkup;ORD.Out[Count].Priority;Connection;ORD.Out[Count].Instrument;ORD.Out[Count].Currency

			#Case
			'CheckL2BookL2' // Check the Book in L2
				#Call;#Priority;#Connection;#Instrument;#currency
				DeskReg.CHCKL2Book;ORD.Out[Count].Priority;Connection;ORD.Out[Count].Instrument;ORD.Out[Count].Currency


			#Case
			'CheckL2BookBW' // Check the Book in BookWindow
				#Call;#Priority;#Connection
				DeskReg.CHCKL2BookFW;ORD.Out[Count].Priority;Connection
				
			#Case
			'CheckL2Book' // Check the Book in L2 & BookWindow
				#Call;#Priority;#Connection;#Instrument;#currency
				DeskReg.CHCKL2Book;ORD.Out[Count].Priority;Connection;ORD.Out[Count].Instrument;ORD.Out[Count].Currency

				#Call;#Priority;#Connection
				DeskReg.CHCKL2BookFW;ORD.Out[Count].Priority;Connection
				
			#Case
			'CheckL1BookL1' // Check the Book in L1
				#Call;#Priority;#Connection;#Instrument;#currency
				DeskReg.CHCKL1BookL1;ORD.Out[Count].Priority;Connection;ORD.Out[Count].Instrument;ORD.Out[Count].Currency
				
			#Case
			'CheckL1BookIL' // Check the Book in InstrumentList
				#Call;#Priority;#Connection;#Instrument;#currency
				DeskReg.CHCKL1BookFW;ORD.Out[Count].Priority;Connection;ORD.Out[Count].Instrument;ORD.Out[Count].Currency

			#Case
			'CheckL1Book' // Check the Book in L1 & InstrumentList
				#Call;#Priority;#Connection;#Instrument;#currency
				DeskReg.CHCKL1BookL1;ORD.Out[Count].Priority;Connection;ORD.Out[Count].Instrument;ORD.Out[Count].Currency

				#Call;#Priority;#Connection;#Instrument;#currency
				DeskReg.CHCKL1BookFW;ORD.Out[Count].Priority;Connection;ORD.Out[Count].Instrument;ORD.Out[Count].Currency

			#Case
			'CheckBBOnTH' // Check BBOnTH, Check BBO, Check TH
				#Off;#Call;#Connection;#Instrument;#currency
				0;DeskReg.CHCKL2BBO;Connection;ORD.Out[Count].Instrument;ORD.Out[Count].Currency

				#Off;#Call;#Connection;#Instrument;#currency
				0;DeskReg.CHCKL2TH;Connection;ORD.Out[Count].Instrument;ORD.Out[Count].Currency

				#Off;#Call;#Connection;#Instrument;#currency
				0;DeskReg.CHCKL1BBO;Connection;ORD.Out[Count].Instrument;ORD.Out[Count].Currency

		//Saves
			#Case
			'SaveWU' // Check the Book
				#Call;#Priority;#NCase;#Connection
				DeskReg.SaveWU;ORD.Out[Count].Priority;NCase;Connection


			#Case
			'SaveBookL1' // Check the Book
				#Call;#Priority;#NCase;#Connection;#Instrument;#currency
				DeskReg.SaveBookL1;ORD.Out[Count].Priority;NCase;Connection;ORD.Out[Count].Instrument;ORD.Out[Count].Currency	


			#Case
			'SaveBookL2' // Check the Book
				#Call;#Priority;#NCase;#Connection;#Instrument;#currency
				DeskReg.SaveBookL2;ORD.Out[Count].Priority;NCase;Connection;ORD.Out[Count].Instrument;ORD.Out[Count].Currency	

		//Other
			#Case
			'Precondition' // MassCancel, Bid, Offer, AgrrOffer, MassCancel
				#Call;#Size;#Price;#Connection;#Instrument;#currency
				DeskReg.PreTrade;ORD.Out[Count].Size;ORD.Out[Count].Price;Connection;ORD.Out[Count].Instrument;ORD.Out[Count].Currency
				
				
			#Case
			'Wait' // Trade
				#Call;#Time
				DeskReg.Waiting;ORD.Out[Count].Time


			#Case
			'SelectCurrency' // Switch currency
				#Call;#Connection;#currency
				DeskReg.CurL1;Connection;ORD.Out[Count].Currency
				
				
			#Case
			'SwitchUserL1' // Switch user
				#Call;#Connection;#Trader
				DeskReg.TraderL1;Connection;ORD.Out[Count].Trader
				
				
			#Case
			'SwitchUserL2' // Switch user
				#Call;#Connection;#Trader;#Instrument;#currency
				DeskReg.TraderL2;Connection;ORD.Out[Count].Trader;ORD.Out[Count].Instrument;ORD.Out[Count].Currency
				
				
			#Case
			'SwitchUserFW' // Switch user
				#Call;#Connection;#Trader
				DeskReg.TraderFW;Connection;ORD.Out[Count].Trader
				
				
			#Case
			'SwitchUserWU' // Switch user
				#Call;#Connection;#Trader
				DeskReg.TraderWU;Connection;ORD.Out[Count].Trader
				
				
			#Case
			'SwitchUserAuc' // Switch user
				#Call;#Connection;#Trader
				DeskReg.TraderAuc;Connection;ORD.Out[Count].Trader
				
				
			#Case
			'Disconnect' // Disconnect ethernet
				#Call
				DeskReg.Disconnect
				
				
			#Case
			'Connect' // Connect ethernet
				#Call
				DeskReg.Connect
				
				
			#Case
			'Reconnect' // Reconnect ethernet
				#Call;#Time
				DeskReg.Reconnect;Time
				
				
			#Case
			'Logout' // Logout user
				#Call;#Connection
				DeskReg.Logout;Connection
				
				
		#EndSwitch

	#EndSubCase

#EndNameSpace
